            <div class="column-center-inner">
             <div class="main section" id="main">
              <div class="widget Blog" id="Blog1">
               <div class="blog-posts hfeed">
                <!-- google_ad_section_start(name=default) -->
                <div class="date-outer">
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry">
                    <a name="23246025765920153">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     Mason Jar Roundup
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-23246025765920153">
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/48529410@N07/5386030275/" title="mason jar collage by Maker Mama, on Flickr">
                       <img alt="ideas-for-mason-jars" height="295" src="http://farm6.static.flickr.com/5213/5386030275_3dd52eee83_z.jpg" title="" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      I finally put the jars to good use! There are still more out in the garage, but here's what I did with these ones:
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/48529410@N07/5385554119/" title="notions jar by Maker Mama, on Flickr">
                       <img alt="ideas-for-mason-jars" height="640" src="http://farm6.static.flickr.com/5215/5385554119_fa1b606554_z.jpg" title="" width="424"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <b>
                       1. Notion Jar
                      </b>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      I used a couple jars to display some crafty eye candy on my sewing table. I picked up a stash of sewing goodies at a garage last fall, but they've been sitting in a shoe box until now.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/48529410@N07/5385552199/" title="pincushion jar by Maker Mama, on Flickr">
                       <img alt="crafts-with-mason-jars" height="640" src="http://farm6.static.flickr.com/5215/5385552199_7feff39a41_z.jpg" title="" width="424"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <b>
                       2. Pincushion
                      </b>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      I originally found this idea in
                      <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Martha-Stewarts-Encyclopedia-Sewing-Fabric/dp/0307450589?ie=UTF8&amp;tag=booksforbread&amp;link_code=btl&amp;camp=213689&amp;creative=392969" target="_blank">
                       Martha Stewart's Encyclopedia of Sewing and Fabric Crafts
                      </a>
                      and I couldn't wait to make one of my own! It's a great way of using up your favorite scraps and I'm thinking of making some as gifts for my crafty friends. You can also find the tutorial on Martha's website
                      <a href="http://www.marthastewart.com/good-things/sewing-kit-in-a-jar">
                       here
                      </a>
                      .
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/48529410@N07/5385550363/" title="soap jar by Maker Mama, on Flickr">
                       <img alt="crafts-with-mason-jars" height="640" src="http://farm6.static.flickr.com/5218/5385550363_8c4e771e0b_z.jpg" title="" width="424"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <b>
                       3. Soap Dispenser
                      </b>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      I've been needing to upgrade our much-used plastic dispensers and this was super-easy to make! You can use the pump from any bottle and just cut the tube to fit your jar. I hammered a nail through the lid to make a hole large enough to fit the pump.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <b>
                      </b>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <b>
                      </b>
                      <a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/48529410@N07/5386157908/" title="rock jar by Maker Mama, on Flickr">
                       <img alt="ideas-for-mason-jars" height="640" src="http://farm6.static.flickr.com/5212/5386157908_a8aa13ab35_z.jpg" title="" width="424"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <b>
                       4. Memento Jar
                      </b>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      I can't go to the beach without combing the shore for souvenirs, and I found these rocks with my husband during our honeymoon in Washington state. I didn't have enough to fill a bowl or vase, but a jar is just right for a small collection.
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      Here are some other upcycled jar ideas from across the web:
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://farm4.static.flickr.com/3016/2569554631_0a914e505f_o.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">

                <script type="text/javascript">
                 document.doAT = function(cl)
{
        var myclass = new RegExp('hentry');
        var myTitleContainer = new RegExp('post-title');
        var myPostContent = new RegExp('post-footer');
        var elem = this.getElementsByTagName('div');
        for (var i = 0; i &lt; elem.length; i++) 
        {
            var classes = elem[i].className;
            if (myclass.test(classes)) 
            {
                var container = elem[i];
                for (var b = 0; b &lt; container.childNodes.length; b++)
                {
                    var item = container.childNodes[b].className;
                    if (myTitleContainer.test(item))
                    {
                        var link = container.childNodes[b].getElementsByTagName('a');
                        if (typeof(link[0]) != 'undefined')
                        {
                            var url = link[0].href;
                            var title = link[0].innerHTML;
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            var url = document.url;
                            var title =  container.childNodes[b].innerHTML;
                        }
                        if (typeof(url) == 'undefined'|| url == 'undefined' ){
                            url = window.location.href;
                        }
                    var singleq = new RegExp("'", 'g');
                    var doubleq = new RegExp('"', 'g');                                                                                                                                                                                                                          
                    title = title.replace(singleq, '&#39;', 'gi');
                    title = title.replace(doubleq, '&#34;', 'gi');
                    
                    }
                    if (myPostContent.test(item))
                    {
                        var footer = container.childNodes[b];
                    }
                }
                var n = document.createElement('div');
                var at = "&lt;div class='addthis_toolbox addthis_default_style addthis_32x32_style' addthis:title='"+title+"' addthis:url='"+encodeURI(url)+"'   &gt; &lt;a class='addthis_button_preferred_1'&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;a class='addthis_button_preferred_2'&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;a class='addthis_button_preferred_3'&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;a class='addthis_button_preferred_4'&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;a class='addthis_button_compact'&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;a class='addthis_counter addthis_bubble_style'&gt;&lt;/a&gt; &lt;/div&gt; ";
                n.innerHTML = at;
                container.insertBefore(n , footer);
            }
        }
    return true;
};

document.doAT('hentry');
